    <script>
    var currentWebProtocol = "https";

    var hasInput = false;
    function setQuestion(){
        if ($("#searchQuestion").val() == 'Buscar'){
            $("#searchQuestion").val('');
            hasInput = true;
        }
    }

    function questionBlur(){
        var question = $("#searchQuestion").val();
        if (question == '' || question == 'Buscar'){
            hasInput = false;
            $("#searchQuestion").val('Buscar');
        }else{
            //[FBATGU-1148] when searchQuestion has value, hasInput is ture
            hasInput = true;
        }
    }

    function typeAheadCallBack(){

    }

    function search(){
        var question = $("#searchQuestion").val();
        if((question == '') || (!hasInput) || question.length<2){
            alert('Ingresa la palabra, producto o código de lo que quieres buscar.');
            return false;
        }else
            return true;
    }
        $(document).ready(function(){
            var question = $("#searchQuestion").val();
            if (question != '' && question != 'Buscar'){
                hasInput = true;
            }

            var maxTypeahead = $("#maxTypeahead").val();
            var group = $("#group").val();
            var count = maxTypeahead * group;

            var typeAheadInfo = {isSearch:"true",maxTypeahead:count};

            if($('#enable_typeahead')!=null && $('#enable_typeahead').val()){
                if(currentWebProtocol === "http"){
                    $("#searchQuestion").autocomplete("/falabella-co/cartridges/typeAhead/typeaheadResults.jsp",{extraParams:typeAheadInfo,selectFirst:false,clickCallBack:typeAheadCallBack});
                }
                else{
                    $("#searchQuestion").autocomplete("/falabella-co/myaccount/typeahead/typeaheadResults.jsp",{extraParams:typeAheadInfo,selectFirst:false,clickCallBack:typeAheadCallBack});
                }
            }
        });
	</script>

	function setNovioId(flag){
		$("#novioId").val(flag);
	}
	function checkInputIsValid(){
		var isValid=true;
		var month=$("#selectMonth").val();
		var year=$("#selectYear").val();
		var validateCode=$("#validationCodeInput").val();
		var code=$("#codeInput").val();
		$('#errorMsg').html("");
		if(month!=""&&year==""||month==""&&year!=""){
			isValid=false;
			var errorMessage = "por favor, introduzca la fecha completa";
			$('#errorMsg').html(errorMessage);
			return isValid;
		}
		if(validateCode!=""&&code==""||validateCode==""&&code!=""){
			isValid=false;
			$('#errorMsg').html("por favor, introduzca el código completo");
			return isValid;
		}
		var nameRegex=/^[a-zA-ZáéíóúÁÉÍÓÚüÜñÑ0-9 ,\\-]*$/;
		var novioNameHome = $("#novioNameHome").val();
		if(!nameRegex.test(novioNameHome)){
			isValid = false;
			$("#errorMsg").html("El nombre es no válido.");
		}
		return isValid;
	}
	function checkInputValue(obj){
		var nameRegex=/^[a-zA-ZáéíóúÁÉÍÓÚüÜñÑ0-9 ,\\-]*$/;
		var flag=nameRegex.test(obj.value);
		if(!flag){
			$('#errorMsg').html("El nombre es no válido.");
			canSaveFlag=false;
		}else{
			$('#errorMsg').html("");
			canSaveFlag=true;
		}
	}
	function validatext(entrada) { 
	     tecla = (document.all) ? entrada.keyCode : entrada.which; 
	     if (tecla==8) return true;  //Tecla de retroceso (para poder borrar)                
	     if (tecla==0) return true;  //Tecla de tabular (para poder saltar entr los campos del formularios)
	     var patron = /\d/;
	       
	     aux = String.fromCharCode(tecla); 
	     return patron.test(aux); 
	}
	function clearInputValues(){
			$("#novioName").val("");
			$("#selectMonth").val("");
			$("#selectYear").val("");
			$("#codeInput").val("");
			$("#validationCodeInput").val("");
	}
	function setInputValue(suffix){
		$("#novioName").val($("#novioName"+suffix).val());
		$("#novioId").val($("#noviaId"+suffix).prop("checked"));
		$("#selectMonth").val($("#selectMonth"+suffix).val());
		$("#selectYear").val($("#selectYear"+suffix).val());
		$("#codeInput").val($("#codeInput"+suffix).val());
		$("#validationCodeInput").val($("#validationCodeInput"+suffix).val());
	}
	function searchNovios(suffix,id,url){
		setInputValue(suffix);
		var valid=checkInputIsValid();
		if(!valid){
			clearInputValues();
			return ;
		}
		var httpOrHttps = "";
			if("https" == httpOrHttps){
			 	url="/falabella-co/myaccount/includes/weddingSearch.jsp";
			}else{
				url="/falabella-co/browse/includes/weddingSearch.jsp"
			}
		
		var loginOptions = {
				url:url,
		      type:"POST",
		      success:function (data) {
		      	   $("#errorMsg").html("");
			       var errorMsg = $(data).find("#message").html();
				   $("#errorMsg").html(errorMsg);
				   $("#noviaIdHome").prop("checked",true);
				   if(errorMsg==null || errorMsg==""){
			       		parent.$("#"+id).colorbox({open:true});
			       }else{
			    	   var omnitureMsg = {
	    	            	omnitureBreadcrumbs:"Listas de Novios",
	    	            	omnitureS_prop12:$.trim(errorMsg)
	    	           };
	    	           omnitureMessageSend(omnitureMsg);
			       }
		      }, 
		      error:function (XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrown) {
		      }
	      }
	      $.ajaxSetup({contentType: "application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=utf-8"});
	      $("#novioSearchId").ajaxSubmit(loginOptions);
	}
</script>

		function saveCurrency(){
			$("#currencyCode").val($("#selecciona-moneda").val());
			$("#saveCurrencyForm").ajaxSubmit({type:"POST",async: false,success:successSaveCurrency,url:"/falabella-co/includes/currencySaveSuccess.jsp"}); 
		}
		function successSaveCurrency(data){
			var mensajeErrorCurrency = $.trim(data);
			if(mensajeErrorCurrency.length==0||mensajeErrorCurrency==""){
				window.location.reload();
			}else{
				$("#showCurrencyMessage").html(mensajeErrorCurrency);
				$("#showSuccess").html("");
			}
		}

    function checkCookieByName(cookieName){
        var documentCookies = document.cookie.split("; ");
        for (var i = 0, l = documentCookies.length; i < l; i++) {
            var parts = documentCookies[i].split("=");
            if(cookieName == parts[0]){
                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }

    function ajaxCallForFirstNameAndCartQuantity() {
        $.ajax({
             async: false,
             type: "POST",
             url: context+"/includes/ajaxFirstNameAndCartQuantity.jsp",
             dataType:"json",
             success: function(data){
                 if(data !=null && data != ""){
                     var firstName = data.ajaxHeaderFirstName;
         firstName=$.trim(firstName);
         if(firstName !=null && firstName != ""){
                 $("#freshLogin").html("Bienvenido!&nbsp;<a href='/falabella-co/myaccount/homeZP.jsp' rel='nofollow'><span id='greeting' class='linkSubrayado'>"+decodeURI(firstName)+"</span></a>&nbsp;o&nbsp;<a onclick='javascript:logout();return false;' href='#' rel='nofollow'><span class='linkSubrayado'>Cerrar sesi\u00f3n</span></a>");
         }
                     var quantity = data.ajaxHeaderCartQuantity;
                     if(quantity > 0){
                     $("#headQuantity").html(quantity+"&nbsp;&nbsp;productos");
                     }
                 }
             }
         });
    }

    $(function(){
        if(checkCookieByName("DYN_USER_ID")){// only for the logged-in users

    if (!(typeof useDynamicDataCookie == "undefined") && useDynamicDataCookie) {

        //Here need to make an ajax call always when the referer url is login or register page.
        var isRefererLoginPage = false;
        var referrerUrl =  document.referrer;
        isRefererLoginPage = referrerUrl == '' || referrerUrl.indexOf('loginForm.jsp') > -1 || referrerUrl.indexOf('register.jsp') > -1;
        if(isRefererLoginPage){
          ajaxCallForFirstNameAndCartQuantity();
        }else{
        //fetch data from another cookie
        var documentCookies = document.cookie.split("; ");
        for (var i = 0, l = documentCookies.length; i < l; i++) {
            var parts = documentCookies[i].split("=");
            if ("DYNAMIC_DATA_COOKIE" == parts[0]) {
            var dynamicDataCookieValue = parts[1].split("*");
            var firstName = dynamicDataCookieValue[0];
            if (firstName != null && firstName != "") {
                firstName = $.trim(firstName);
                $("#freshLogin").html("Bienvenido!&nbsp;<a href='/falabella-co/myaccount/homeZP.jsp' rel='nofollow'><span id='greeting' class='linkSubrayado'>" + decodeURI(firstName) + "</span></a>&nbsp;o&nbsp;<a onclick='javascript:logout();return false;' href='#' rel='nofollow'><span class='linkSubrayado'>Cerrar sesi\u00f3n</span></a>");
                // $("#greeting").html(firstName);
            }
            var quantity = dynamicDataCookieValue[1];
            if (quantity > 0) {
                $("#headQuantity").html(quantity + "&nbsp;&nbsp;productos");
            }
            break;
            }
        }
        }
    } else { //post to ATG , get the fresh data
            ajaxCallForFirstNameAndCartQuantity();
           }
  }
  else if (checkCookieByName("loyaltyCookie")) { // SSN-1126 - for loyalty site users
      if (!(typeof useDynamicDataCookie == "undefined") && useDynamicDataCookie) { //fetch data from another cookie
        var documentCookies = document.cookie.split("; ");
        for (var i = 0, l = documentCookies.length; i < l; i++) {
          var parts = documentCookies[i].split("=");
          if ("DYNAMIC_DATA_COOKIE" == parts[0]) {

            var quantity = dynamicDataCookieValue[1];
            if (quantity > 0) {
              $("#headQuantity").html(quantity + "&nbsp;&nbsp;productos");
            }
          }

        }
      }else { //post to ATG , get the fresh data

      $.ajax({
        async: false,
        type: "POST",
        url: context + "/includes/ajaxFirstNameAndCartQuantity.jsp",
        dataType: "json",
        success: function(data) {
          if (data != null && data != "") {
            var quantity = data.ajaxHeaderCartQuantity;
            if (quantity > 0) {
              $("#headQuantity").html(quantity + "&nbsp;&nbsp;productos");
            }
          }
        }
      });
    }
  }
  else

	    //SSN-1700 Problem auto_login=0 user

	        isRefererLoginPage = referrerUrl == '' || referrerUrl.indexOf('loginForm.jsp') > -1 || referrerUrl.indexOf('register.jsp') > -1;

	(new RegExp("\/" + tagContext + "\/index.jsp")).test(url) ||
	(new RegExp("\/" + tagContext + "\/category\/")).test(url) ||
	(new RegExp("\/" + tagContext + "\/search\/")).test(url) ||
	(new RegExp("\/" + tagContext + "\/product\/")).test(url) ||

			{event: "setSiteType", type: "d"}

			);

                               });
                       });
			local_criteo_array.push(
				{event: "viewBasket", item: items}
			);
		} else if((new RegExp("\/" + tagContext + "\/checkout\/submitOrderSuccess.jsp")).test(url)){
		
			lines = s.products.split(";");
			if (lines.length > 3){
				lines.splice(lines.length - 4, 1);
			}
			line_items = [];
			for(index = 0; index < lines.length; index = index + 3)
			{
				   item = {};
				   item.id = lines[index];
				   item.quantity = lines[index + 1];
				   item.price = Number(lines[index + 2].replace(",",""));
				   line_items.push(item);
			}
			local_criteo_array.push( 
						{ event: "setSiteType", type: "d" },
						{ event: "trackTransaction" , id: s.purchaseID,
							deduplication: '1', item: line_items
			});
		}
    //    	console.log(local_criteo_array);
		window.criteo_q = window.criteo_q || [];
    	window.criteo_q.push(local_criteo_array);
    }

/**
 * 
 * @param {Element} element anchor element
 * @returns {Boolean} true if out of domain
 */
function isOutOfDomain(element) {
    if (element && element.tagName === 'A') {
        var url = element.href;
        url = url.indexOf('?') != -1 ? url.substring(0, url.indexOf('?')) : url;
        if (/falabella.com/.test(url)) {
            return false;
        } else if (/mi-cuenta\/giftcards/.test(url)) {
            return true;
        }
        return true;
    }
    return false;
}

var ui = {
    isSLP: function() {
        return true;
    },
    str: function str() {
        return 'T|x|x|x|x|x|x|x|x';

    },
    approvedTrackClick: function approvedTrackClick(menulink) {
        var isMenuLink = false;
        if (/(ThirdLevelItems|SecondLevelItems|ToggleThirdCategories|thirdLevelMenu)/.test(menulink.className) || menulink && menulink.parentElement && /secondLevelMenu__/.test(menulink.parentElement.className) || menulink.closest('[class*="thirdLevelMenu__mobile"]')) {
            isMenuLink = true;
        }
        if (!isMenuLink)
            return;
        var finalCondition = false;
        finalCondition = isMenuLink;
        return finalCondition;
    },
    firstLevelDescription: function() {
        var windowW = window.screen.width < 1024;
        if (ui.isSLP()) {
            var menuItems = document.querySelectorAll('[class*="firstLevelMenu__"] li');
            menuItemsArr = [].slice.apply(menuItems);
            var a = menuItemsArr.find(function(element, i) {
                if (/active/.test(element.className)) {
                    return element;
                }
            });
            return windowW ? document.querySelector('[class*="firstLevelMenu__title--active"]').textContent.trim() : a.textContent.trim();

        }
    },
    firstLevelPosition: function() {

                if (/display/.test(element.className)) {
                    index = i;
                }
            });

    secondLevelDescription: function(theParent) {

        var columnOrder = function() {

var myInterval = setInterval(
  function() {
    
      // Get button login Facebook
      var loginFacebook = document.querySelector(".btnFacebookLogin");
    
      if (loginFacebook) {
        
        // Get father button login Facebook
        var fatherLoginFacebook = loginFacebook.parentElement;
        fatherLoginFacebook.removeChild(loginFacebook);

        // Get all span with text into form login
        var spanTexts = document.querySelectorAll('span.bajadaLogin');

        // Fin into array spans text equals "Ingresa con tu perfil de Facebook"
        spanTexts.forEach(function (el) {
          
          if (el.innerText === 'Ingresa con tu perfil de Facebook') {
            el.parentElement.removeChild(el);
          }
        });
      }
